title="NASA Delays Artemis II Mission: What You Need to Know About the New Launch Date and Its Impact on Lunar Exploration 18" data-eio="l"></noscript>			</a><div class="entry-summary"><p>NASA&#8217;s Artemis II lunar mission has faced a setback, with the launch date now pushed back from March 6 to April. This change comes in light of a failure in the helium flow system of the Space Launch System (SLS) rocket, critical for engine purging and fuel tank pressurization. With the second dress rehearsal successful,&#8230;</p><p class="more-link-wrap"><a href="https://jcorcione.com/nasa-delays-artemis-ii-mission-what-you-need-to-know-about-the-new-launch-date-and-its-impact-on-lunar-exploration/" class="more-link">Read More<span class="screen-reader-text"> &ldquo;NASA Delays Artemis II Mission: What You Need to Know About the New Launch Date and Its Impact on Lunar Exploration&rdquo;</span> &raquo;</a></p><div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled"><div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon sd-sharing"><h3 class="sd-title">Share this:</h3><div class="sd-content"><ul><li class="share-twitter"><a rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer"
